		SheetMetal=7,
		Hinge=2,
		PaintGrey=2,
		BlowTorch=10,
		keep Paintbrush,
        keep [Recipe.GetItemTypes.Screwdriver],
        Result:Grey_Military_Crate4,
		Time:800.0, 
		NeedToBeLearn:true,
		Category:Containers, 
		Tooltip:Tooltip_CContainer_Tier_4,
		SkillRequired:MetalWelding=4,
		Sound:Hammering,
 	}
